Deck Lists: Top Block Constructed Lists
=======================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 29, 2010 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











Presented here are the deck lists of players who recorded 18 or more points in the 10 Swiss rounds of Block Constructed play at Pro Tour-San Juan. Deck lists for Simon Görtzen (19 points), Aras Aziz (18), Christian Bateman (18), and Davide Brambilla (18) unavailable at time of publication.






#### Ben Hayes, 30 points


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
